Question:
[math]\tan \theta+\cot \theta=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{2}{\sin 2 \theta}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{2}{\cos 2 \theta}[/math]
C. [math]\sin 2 \theta[/math]
D. [math]\cos 2 \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}+\frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}=\frac{\sin ^{2} \theta+\cos ^{2} \theta}{\sin \theta \cos \theta} . \\\Rightarrow \frac{2}{2 \sin \theta \cos \theta}=\frac{2}{\sin 2 \theta}\end{array}[/math]

Question #264 (ID: 472820)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sec \theta+\tan \theta=x[/math] হলে [math]\frac{\sin \theta+1}{\sin \theta-1}[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{x^{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{-1}{x^{2}}[/math]
C. [math]x^{2}[/math]
D. [math]-x^{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sec \theta+\tan \theta=x\\\Rightarrow \frac{1+\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}=x \Rightarrow \frac{(1+\sin \theta)^{2}}{\cos ^{2} \theta}=x^{2}\\\Rightarrow \frac{1+\sin \theta}{1-\sin \theta}=x^{2} \Rightarrow \frac{\sin \theta+1}{\sin \theta-1}=-x^{2}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #265 (ID: 472821)

Question:
[math]\cot \theta=-\frac{4}{3}[/math] এবং [math]0 \leq \theta \leq \pi[/math] হলে [math]\frac{\sec (-\theta)+\cos \theta}{\sin \theta-\tan \theta}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{20}{27}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{27}{20}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{-41}{27}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{-27}{41}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cot \theta=\frac{-4}{3}[/math]
 এবং [math]0 \leq \theta \leq \pi[/math]
 হলে[math]\begin{array}{l}\sec (-\theta)=\sec \theta=\frac{5}{-4} \\\cos \theta=\frac{-4}{5} \\\sin \theta=\frac{3}{5} \\\tan \theta=\frac{-3}{4} \\\therefore \frac{\sec (-\theta)+\cos \theta}{\sin \theta-\tan \theta}=\frac{-\frac{5}{4}-\frac{4}{5}}{\frac{3}{5}+\frac{3}{4}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\frac{-25-16}{20}}{\frac{27}{20}}=\frac{-41}{27} \\\end{array}[/math]

[Image]


Explanation:

Question #268 (ID: 472804)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2008-2009 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
6 একক দৈর্ঘ্যবিশিষ্ট একটি জ্যা [math](x-3)^{2}+(y-4)^{2}=25[/math] বৃত্তের কেন্দ্রে কত কোণ তৈরী করে?

Options:
ক. [math]\sin ^{-1}(6 / 5)[/math]
খ. [math]\sin ^{-1}(3 / 5)[/math]
গ. [math]2 \sin ^{-1} \cdot(3 / 5)[/math]
ঘ. [math]\tan ^{-1} \frac{6}{5}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
Hints: জ্যা এর ওপর কেন্দ্র হতে অঙ্কিত লম্ব উক্ত জ্যাকে সমদ্বিখন্ডিত করে।AB = 64; একক CD [math]\perp[/math]
AB বলে AD = DB.:. AD=34 এককআবার [math](x-3)^{2}+(y-4)^{2}=25[/math]
 .বৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ = 5 = AC [math]\triangle \mathrm{ADC} \text { তে, } \sin \theta=\frac{A D}{A C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta=\frac{3}{5} \Rightarrow \theta=\sin ^{-1}\left(\frac{3}{5}\right)[/math]
কেন্দ্রস্ত কোণ [math]\angle A C B=\angle A C D+\angle B C D[/math]
 [math]=\theta+\theta=2 \theta=2 \sin -1\left(\frac{3}{5}\right)[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: প্রথমে △ ADC সমকোণী ত্রিভূজ নিয়ে কাজ করে B এর মান বের করা হয়েছে। এরপর কেন্দ্রস্থ কোণ ∠ ACB বের করা হয়েছে।

খ. [math]10^{3}[/math]

ঘ. [math]330.15[/math]

 [math]=6331.18 \mathrm{~km}[/math]

Question #276 (ID: 472798)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2010-2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan ^{2} \theta=3 \operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta-1[/math] হলে, [math]\tan \theta=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]0.3[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{2}{3}[/math]
D. [math]\pm \sqrt{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\tan ^{2} \theta=3 \operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta-1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]=3+3 \cot ^{2} \theta-1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]=2+\frac{3}{\tan ^{2} \theta}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(\tan ^{2} \theta\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=3+2 \tan ^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(\tan ^{2} \theta\right)^{2}-2 \tan ^{2} \theta-3[/math]
 [math]=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(\tan ^{2} \theta-3\right)[/math]
 [math]\left(\tan ^{2} \theta+1\right)[/math]
 [math]=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \theta= \pm \sqrt{3},[/math]
 [math]\tan \theta= \pm \sqrt{-1}[/math]
 [গ্রহণযোগ্য নয়]

Explanation:

Question #279 (ID: 472801)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2009-2010 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
n বাহুবিশিষ্ট কোন সুষম বহুভূজের যেকোন বহিঃস্থ কোণের মান 72° হলে n এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. 4
খ. 5
গ. 6
ঘ. 8


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
Hints: সুষম বহুভুজের প্রত্যেকটা বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য সমান, তাই প্রতিটি কোণের মানও সমান । আর যে কোনো বহুভুজের বহিঃস্থ কোণগুলোর যোগফল [math]360°[/math]
 ।Solve : যেহেতু বহিঃস্থ কোণগুলোর সমষ্টি [math]360°[/math]
 এবং প্রতিটি বহিঃস্থ কোণের মান 72º, সেহেতু কোণের সংখ্যা [math]=\frac{360}{72}=5[/math]
টিআর যতগুলো কোণ, বাহুর সংখ্যাও ততগুলো। অর্থাৎ [math]n = 5[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: তিন বাহুবিশিষ্ট সুষম বহুভুজ অর্থাৎ সমবাহু ত্রিভুজের প্রতিটি অন্তঃস্থ কোণের মান 60°, বহিঃস্থ কোণের মান 120°চার বাহুবিশিষ্ট সুষম চতুর্ভূজ অর্থাৎ বর্গের প্রতিটি অন্তঃস্থ কোণের মান 90, বহিঃস্থ কোণের মানও 90°পাঁচ বাহুবিশিষ্ট সুষম পঞ্চভুজের প্রতিটি অন্তঃস্থ কোণের মান 108º, বহিঃস্থ কোণের মান 72°

Question #285 (ID: 472790)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University, Gopalganj (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan A=x[/math] হলে [math]\sin 2 \mathrm{~A}+\tan 2 \mathrm{~A}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{4 x}{1-x^{4}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{4 x^{2}}{1-x^{3}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{x}{1-x^{2}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{4 x}{1-x^{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sin 2 A+\tan 2 A=[/math]
 [math]\frac{2 \tan A}{1+\tan ^{2} A}[/math]
 [math]+\frac{2 \tan A}{1-\tan ^{2} A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 x}{1+x^{2}}[/math]
 [math]+\frac{2 x}{1-x^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{4 x}{\left(1-x^{4}\right)}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #291 (ID: 472767)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Pabna University of Science and Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin \theta[/math] কে [math]\cot \theta[/math] এর মাধ্যমে প্রকাশ কর-

Options:
ক. [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{1+\cot ^{2} \theta}}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2+\cot ^{2} \theta}}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{1+\cot ^{2} \theta}}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{1-\cot ^{2} \theta}}[/math]
ঙ. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2-\cot ^{2} \theta}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sin ^{2} \theta+\cos ^{2} \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \theta+\frac{\cos ^{2} \theta}{\sin ^{2} \theta}[/math]
 [math]\times \sin ^{2} \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin ^{2}[/math]
 [math]\theta\left(1+\cot ^{2} \theta\right)=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{1+\cot ^{2} \theta}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{1+\cot ^{2} \theta}}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\cos ^{4} \theta-\sin ^{4} \theta=?[/math]

B. [math]\cos 2 \theta[/math]
C. [math]2 \cos 2 \theta[/math]
D. [math]2 \operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos ^{4} \theta-\sin ^{4} \theta[/math]
 [math]=\left(\cos ^{2} \theta-\sin ^{2} \theta\right)[/math]
 [math]\left(\cos ^{2} \theta+\sin ^{2} \theta\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos 2 \theta \times 1[/math]
 [math]=\cos 2 \theta[/math]

Question #294 (ID: 472770)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University, Gopalganj (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sec \theta+\tan \theta=4[/math] হলে [math]\tan \theta=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{15}{8}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{17}{8}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{13}{8}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{11}{8}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\frac{1}{\cos \theta}+\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]=4 \text { Or, } 1+\sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=4 \cos \theta \text { Or, } 1^{2}+2 \sin \theta+\sin ^{2} \theta=16 \cos ^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]\text { Or, } 17 \sin ^{2} \theta+2 \sin \theta-15[/math]
 [math]=0 \text { Or, } 17 \sin ^{2}[/math]
 [math]\theta+17 \sin \theta-15 \sin \theta-15=0[/math]
 [math]\text { Or, } 17 \sin[/math]
 [math]\theta(\sin \theta+1)-15(\sin \theta+1)=0 \quad[/math]
 [math]\text { Or, }(\sin \theta+1)[/math]
 [math](17 \sin \theta-15)[/math]
 [math]=0[/math]
 [math]\text { if } \sin \theta=-1;[/math]
 [math]\text { then,}\tan \theta=\infty \quad[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta=\frac{15}{17}[/math]
 [math]\tan \theta=\frac{15}{8}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
বৃত্তের ব্যাসের সমান চাপ কেন্দ্রে যে কোণ তৈরি করে তার পরিমাণ কত রেডিয়ান?

Options:
ক. 1
খ. 2
গ. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
ঙ. [math]\pi[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
Hints: বৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধের সমান চাপ কেন্দ্রে যে কোণ তৈরি করে তাকে বলে 1 রেডিয়ান।Solve : ব্যাসার্ধ হলে, ব্যাস = 2r, r এর সমান চাপ = 1 রেডিয়ান2r এর সমান চাপ = 1×2 রেডিয়ান = 2 রেডিয়ান

Explanation:

Question #298 (ID: 472774)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]2.0 \times 10^{-10}[/math]m দূরত্বে অবস্থিত দুটি ইলেকট্রনের মধ্যে মহাকর্ষ বল এবং তড়িৎ বল উভয়ই ক্রিয়া করে। অভিকর্ষ বলের মান তড়িৎ বলের চেয়ে কতগুণ কম বা বেশি শক্তিশালী?

Options:
ক. [math]10^{42}[/math]গুণ কম
খ. [math]10^{-42}[/math]গুণ কম
গ. [math]10^{42}[/math]গুণ বেশি
ঘ. [math]10^{-42}[/math]গুণ বেশি
ঙ. [math]10^{11}[/math]গুণ বেশি


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\text{Hints: } F_{g}=G \frac{m_{1} \times m_{2}}{r^{2}} ;[/math]
 [math]F_{e}=E \times q ; \text{ অত:পর } \frac{F_{g}}{F_{e}}[/math]
 [math]\text{Solve: } F_{g}=G \frac{m_{1} \times m_{2}}{r^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\left[\mathrm{G}=6.673 \times 10^{-11} \mathrm{Nm}^{2} \mathrm{~kg}^{-}\right.[/math]
 ইলেকট্রনের ভর [math]\left.\mathrm{m}=9.11 \times 10^{-3} \mathrm{~kg}\right][/math]
 [math]=6.673 \times 10^{-11} \times \frac{\left(9.11 \times 10^{-31}\right)^{2}}{\left(2 \times 10^{-10}\right)^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=1.38 \times 10^{-51} \mathrm{~N}[/math]
again [math]\mathrm{F}_{\mathrm{e}}=\mathrm{E} \times \mathrm{q}=9 \times 10^{9} \times \frac{\mathrm{q}}{\mathrm{r}^{2}} \times \mathrm{q}[/math]
 [math]=9 \times 10^{9} \frac{\left(1.6 \times 10^{-19}\right)^{2}}{\left(2 \times 10^{-10}\right)^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=5.76 \times 10^{-9} \mathrm{~N}[/math]
এখন [math]\frac{F_{g}}{F_{e}}=\frac{1.38 \times 10^{-51}}{5.76 \times 10^{-9}}[/math]
 [math]=0.24 \times 10^{-42}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{F}_{\mathrm{g}}[/math]
 [math]=0.24 \times 10^{-42} \times \mathrm{F}_{\mathrm{e}}[/math]


Explanation:
চারটি মৌলিক বলের মধ্যে মহাকর্ষ বল সবচাইতে দুর্বল এবং সবচেয়ে শক্তিশালী বল হচ্ছে সবল নিউক্লিয় বল। চারটি মৌলিক বল নিম্নরূপ:i) মহাকর্ষ বল (গ্রাভিটন নামক কণার বিনিময়ে উৎপত্তি হয়)ii) সবল নিউক্লিয় বল (গ্লঅন নামক কণা বিনিময়ে উৎপত্তি হয়)iii) দুর্বল নিউক্লিয় বল (বোসন নামক কণার বিনিময়ে কার্যকর হয়)iv) তড়িৎ চৌম্বক বল (ফোটন নামক কণার বিনিময়ে কার্যকর হয়)

Question #303 (ID: 472779)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University, Gopalganj (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A এর কোন মানের জন্য [math]\cos A \sin \left(A-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)[/math] এর মান বৃহত্তম হয় ?

Options:
ক. [math]\pi / 2[/math]
খ. [math]\pi / 3[/math]
গ. $\pi / 6
ঘ. [math]\pi / 12[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos A \sin (A-\pi / 6)=\frac{1}{2}[2 \cos A \sin (A-\pi / 6)]=\frac{1}{2}\left[\sin (2 A-\pi / 6)-\sin \frac{\pi}{6}\right][/math]
রাশিটি বৃহত্তম হবে যদি [math]\sin (2 \mathrm{~A}-\pi / 6)=1 \Rightarrow(2 \mathrm{~A}-\pi / 6)=\frac{\pi}{2} \quad \therefore \mathrm{A}=\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #306 (ID: 472782)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2020-2021, 2017-2018, 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: Agriculture Cluster Admission System, Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Khulna University (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin \alpha+\operatorname{cosec} \alpha=2[/math] হলে, [math]\sin ^{n} \alpha+\operatorname{cosec}^{n} \alpha[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]2[/math]
B. [math]-2[/math]
C. [math]3[/math]
D. [math]-3[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sin \alpha+\operatorname{cosec} \alpha[/math]
 [math]=2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \alpha+\frac{1}{\sin \alpha}[/math]
 [math]=2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \alpha+1[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \alpha[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \alpha-2 \sin \alpha+1=[/math]
 [math]0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(\sin \alpha-1)^{2}=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \alpha=1[/math]
 এবং [math]\operatorname{cosec} \alpha=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin ^{\mathrm{n}} \alpha+\operatorname{cosec}^{\mathrm{n}} \alpha[/math]
 [math]=1^{\mathrm{n}}+\mathrm{1}^{\mathrm{n}}[/math]
 [math]=1+1=2[/math]


Explanation:

Question #311 (ID: 472761)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2018-2019, 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Chittagong (Unit A), University of Chittagong (Unit A)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sqrt{\frac{1-\sin A}{1+\sin A}}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]cosA[/math]
B. [math]secA + tanA[/math]
C. [math]tanA-secA[/math]
D. [math]secA-tanA[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\sqrt{\frac{1-\sin A}{1+\sin A}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\sin A}{\sqrt{1-\sin ^{2} A}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\sin A}{\sqrt{\cos ^{2} A}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\sin A}{\cos A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\cos A}[/math]
 [math]-\frac{\sin A}{\cos A}[/math]
 [math]=\sec A-\tan A[/math]


Explanation:

Question #312 (ID: 472762)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Question:
Trigonometry শব্দের উৎপত্তি কোন ভাষা থেকে?

Options:
ক. আরবি
খ. সংস্কৃত
গ. গ্রিক
ঘ. ইংরেজি


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
Trigonometry শব্দটি গ্রিক ভাষা থেকে উৎপত্তি

Question:
যদি [math]\operatorname{cos} \theta=\frac{12}{13}[/math] হয়, তাহলে [math]\tan \theta[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]\pm \frac{5}{12}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{25}{144}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{15}{12}[/math]
D. [math]\pm \frac{13}{12}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sin \theta=\sqrt{1-\cos ^{2} \theta}[/math]
 [math]= \pm \frac{5}{13} \quad[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \theta= \pm \frac{5}{12}[/math]

Question #315 (ID: 472759)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022-2023, 2015-2016, 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \theta+\sin \theta=\sqrt{2} \cos \theta[/math] হলে, [math]\cos \theta-\sin \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\cos \theta-\sin \theta[/math]
B. [math]2 \sin \theta[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{2} \sin \theta[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{2 \sin \theta}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos \theta+\sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{2} \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{2} \cos \theta-\cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=(\sqrt{2}-1) \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(\sqrt{2}+1) \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=(\sqrt{2}-1)[/math]
 [math](\sqrt{2}+1) \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sqrt{2} \sin \theta+\sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=\cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \theta-\sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{2} \sin \theta[/math]


Explanation:

Question #318 (ID: 472750)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Jagannath University (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]sine - cost = 0[/math] হলে, [math]\theta[/math] এর ক্ষুদ্রতম ধনাত্মক মান কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\sin \theta-\cos \theta=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \theta-1=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \quad[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]


Explanation:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x=\sin \theta-|\cos \theta|, 0<\theta<\pi[/math] এর লঘুমান এবং গুরুমান যথাক্রমে-

Options:
ক. [math]-2, 2[/math]
খ. [math]-2, 0[/math]
গ. [math]0,1[/math]
ঘ. [math]-1,1[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\mathrm{x}=\sin \theta-|\cos \theta|[/math]
লঘুমান হবে যখন, [math]\sin \theta=0, \cos \theta=1[/math]
লঘুমান [math]x=-1[/math]
গুরুমান হবে যখন, [math]\sin \theta=1, \cos \theta=0[/math]
গুরুমান, [math]x=1[/math]


Explanation:

Question #321 (ID: 472753)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Rajshahi University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
কোন ত্রিভুজের ভূমি সংলগ্ন কোণদ্বয় [math]22.5°[/math] ও [math]112.5°[/math] ও ত্রিভুজের উচ্চতা [math]h[/math] হলে ভূমি কত?

Options:
ক. [math]h[/math]
খ. [math]2h[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{\mathrm{h}}{2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{h}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
ঙ. [math]\text { None }[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:

[Image]
ধরি, ত্রিভুজটির ভূমি x এবং স্থূলকোণ সংলগ্ন অপর বাহু bএখন, [math]b \sin 112.5^{\circ}=h[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow h=\frac{h}{\sin 112.5^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]\text { Sine rule }[/math]
 প্রয়োগ করে, [math]\frac{x}{\sin 15^{\circ}}=[/math]
 [math]\frac{b}{\sin 22.5^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{h}{\sin 1125^{\circ}}}{\sin 22.5^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore x=2 h[/math]


Explanation:

Question #326 (ID: 472747)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Jahangirnagar University (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sec \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta=0[/math] হলে, [math]\cos \theta[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sec \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]-\frac{1}{\sin \theta}[/math]
 [math]=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \theta[/math]
 [math]=1=\tan \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #332 (ID: 472729)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2016-2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Chattogram Veterinary and Animal Sciences University
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin 10^{\circ} \sin 50^{\circ} \sin 70^{\circ}[/math] এর মান হবে -

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{8}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{4}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sin 10^{\circ} \cdot \underbrace{\sin 50^{\circ}}_{=\cos 40^{\circ}} \cdot \underbrace{\sin 70^{\circ}}_{=\cos 20^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\sin 10^{\circ} \cdot \cos 40^{\circ} \cdot \cos 20^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2 \cos 10^{\circ}} \cdot[/math]
 [math][\underbrace{2 \sin 10^{\circ} \cdot \cos 10^{\circ}}_{=\sin 20^{\circ}}] \cdot[/math]
 [math]\cos 40^{\circ} \cdot \cos 20^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4 \cos 10^{\circ}} \cdot[/math]
 [math][\underbrace{2 \sin 20^{\circ} \cdot \cos 20^{\circ}}_{=\sin 40^{\circ}}][/math]
 [math]\cdot \cos 40^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{8 \cos 10^{\circ}} \cdot[\underbrace{2 \sin 40^{\circ} \cdot \cos 40^{\circ}}_{=\sin 80^{\circ}}][/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{8 \cos 10^{\circ}} \cdot \underbrace{\sin 80^{\circ}}_{=\cos 10^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{8}[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #333 (ID: 472730)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2016-2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Jhenidah Government Veterinary College
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan 15^{\circ}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]1-\sqrt{3}[/math]
B. [math]2-\sqrt{3}[/math]
C. [math]1+\sqrt{3}[/math]
D. [math]2+\sqrt{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\text { Simplify } \tan 15^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\tan \left(45-30^{\circ}\right) \\=\frac{\tan 45-\tan 30^{\circ}}{1+\tan 45 \tan 30^{\circ}} \\=\frac{1-\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}{1+1 \times \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}} \\=\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{\sqrt{3}+1} \\=2-\sqrt{3}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #335 (ID: 472732)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2016-2017 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Chittagong (Unit A)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\sin A}{1+\cos A}+\frac{1+\cos A}{\sin A}[/math] এর মান হয়-

Options:
A. [math]2[/math] [math]secA[/math]
B. [math]2[/math] [math]cotA[/math]
C. [math]2[/math] [math]tanA[/math]
D. [math]2[/math] [math]cosecA[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\frac{\sin A}{1+\cos A}+\frac{1+\cos A}{\sin A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin ^{2} A+1+\cos ^{2} A+2 \cos A}{\sin A(1+\cos A)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1+1+2 \cos A}{\sin A(1+\cos A)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2+2 \cos A}{\sin A(1+\cos A)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2(1+\cos A)}{\sin A(1+\cos A)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2}{\sin A}[/math]
 [math]=2 \operatorname{cosec} A[/math]


Explanation:

Question #336 (ID: 472733)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman Science and Technology University, Gopalganj (B Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]y^{2}=2 x^{2}[/math] বক্ররেখার কোন বিন্দুতে স্পর্শকটি [math]4 x-3 y+1=0[/math] সরলরেখার সাথে লম্ব হবে?

Options:
ক. [math]\left(-\frac{1}{8}, \frac{1}{16}\right)[/math]
খ. [math]\left(\frac{1}{8},-\frac{1}{16}\right)[/math]
গ. [math]\left(-\frac{1}{8},-\frac{1}{16}\right)[/math]
ঘ. [math]\left(\frac{1}{8}, \frac{1}{16}\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]y^{2}=2 x^{3}[/math]
 [math]\cdots \cdots[/math]
 [math]\text { (i); } \frac{d y}{d x}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{6 x^{2}}{2 y}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{3 x^{2}}{y}[/math]
 [math]4 x-3 y+1=0[/math]
 রেখার উপর লম্ব রেখার [math]=-\frac{3}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{3 x^{2}}{y}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{3}{4}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow y=-4 x^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow y^{2}=16 x^{4}[/math]
 [math]\cdots \cdots(ii)[/math]
(i) ও (ii) হতে, [math]x=\frac{2}{16}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{8},[/math]
 [math]y=-4 \times \frac{1}{64}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{16}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \text { Ans: }\left(\frac{1}{8},-\frac{1}{16}\right)[/math]


Explanation:

Question #338 (ID: 472735)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022-2023, 2015-2016, 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \theta+\sin \theta=\sqrt{2} \cos \theta[/math] হলে, [math]\cos \theta-\sin \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\cos \theta-\sin \theta[/math]
B. [math]2 \sin \theta[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{2} \sin \theta[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{2 \sin \theta}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos \theta+\sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{2} \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{2} \cos \theta-\cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=(\sqrt{2}-1) \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(\sqrt{2}+1) \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=(\sqrt{2}-1)[/math]
 [math](\sqrt{2}+1) \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sqrt{2} \sin \theta+\sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=\cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \theta-\sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{2} \sin \theta[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{3}{4}[/math] হলে, [math]\frac{\sin \theta-\cos \theta}{\sin \theta+\cos \theta}[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. 7
B. [math]\frac{1}{7}[/math]
C. [math]-\frac{1}{7}[/math]
D. [math]-7[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{3}{4}[/math]
এখানে, [math]\frac{\sin \theta-\cos \theta}{\sin \theta+\cos \theta}=\frac{\tan \theta-1}{\tan \theta+1}[/math]
 [math]\frac{\frac{3}{4}-1}{\frac{3}{4}+1}=[/math]
 [math]\frac{-\frac{1}{4}}{\frac{7}{4}}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{7}[/math]

Question:
[math]\sin A=\frac{1}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\cos B=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math] হলে, [math]\tan A \cdot \tan B[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{2}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{3}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\tan A \cdot \tan B=\frac{1}{\cot A} \cdot \tan B[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \mathrm{~A}-1}}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \sqrt{\sec ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{4-1}}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \sqrt{3-1}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \sqrt{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #356 (ID: 472714)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2020-2021, 2017-2018, 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: Agriculture Cluster Admission System, Jahangirnagar University (A Unit), Khulna University (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin \alpha+\operatorname{cosec} \alpha=2[/math] হলে, [math]\sin ^{n} \alpha+\operatorname{cosec}^{n} \alpha[/math] এর মান-

Options:
A. [math]2[/math]
B. [math]-2[/math]
C. [math]3[/math]
D. [math]-3[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sin \alpha+\operatorname{cosec} \alpha[/math]
 [math]=2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \alpha+\frac{1}{\sin \alpha}[/math]
 [math]=2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \alpha+1[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \alpha[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \alpha-2 \sin \alpha+1=[/math]
 [math]0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(\sin \alpha-1)^{2}=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \alpha=1[/math]
 এবং [math]\operatorname{cosec} \alpha=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin ^{\mathrm{n}} \alpha+\operatorname{cosec}^{\mathrm{n}} \alpha[/math]
 [math]=1^{\mathrm{n}}+\mathrm{1}^{\mathrm{n}}[/math]
 [math]=1+1=2[/math]


Explanation:

Question:

[Image]

A. [math]\frac{\pi}{2} \mathrm{~cm}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{3 \pi}{2} \mathrm{~cm}[/math]
C. [math]\pi \mathrm{cm}[/math]
D. [math]2 \pi \mathrm{cm}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\frac{\pi}{2} \mathrm{~cm}[/math]

Solution:

[Image]

ক. [math]\pi[/math]
খ. [math]2\pi[/math]

Question:
[math]\tan \frac{3 x}{2}[/math] এর মৌলিক পর্যায় কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{2 \pi}{3}[/math]
গ. [math]\pi[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{3 \pi}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\frac{2 \pi}{3}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\tan \mathrm{x}[/math]
 এর মৌলিক পর্যায় [math]\pi[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \frac{3 \mathrm{x}}{2}[/math]
 এর মৌলিক পর্যায় [math]=\frac{\pi}{\frac{3}{2}}=\frac{2 \pi}{3}[/math]

Question:
নিচের উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{5}{8}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{5}{7}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{7}{5}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{8}{5}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{7}{5}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\mathrm{AB}=3, \mathrm{BC}=4[/math]
 হলে, [math]A C=5[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \theta+\cos \phi=\frac{3}{5}+\frac{4}{5}=\frac{7}{5}[/math]

Question #370 (ID: 398387)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]2 A B=B C[/math] হলে [math]\sin \theta=?[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\sin \varphi[/math]
খ. [math]2 \sin \varphi[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{1}{2} \sin \varphi[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{1}{4} \sin \varphi[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]2 \sin \varphi[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sin \theta=\frac{\mathrm{BC}}{\mathrm{AC}}, \sin \phi=\frac{\mathrm{AB}}{\mathrm{AC}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta=\frac{\mathrm{AB}}{\mathrm{AC}}[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{\mathrm{BC}}{\mathrm{AB}}[/math]
 [math]=(\sin \phi) \times 2[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \phi[/math]


Explanation:

[Image]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক

A. i ও ii
B. ii ও iii
C. i ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii

Question #379 (ID: 398375)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \left(\frac{x}{3}+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)[/math] এর পর্যায় কোনটি ?

Options:
A. [math]6 \pi[/math]
B. [math]3 \pi[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]6 \pi[/math]

Solution:
[math]\cos n x[/math]
 এর পর্যায় [math]\frac{2 \pi}{n}, \text { cosine }[/math]
 এর পর্যায় দশা কোণের (এখানে, [math]\left.\frac{\pi}{4}\right)[/math]
 উপর নির্ভরশীল নয়।[math]\therefore[/math]
 পর্যায় [math]=\frac{2 \pi}{\frac{1}{3}}=6 \pi[/math]


Explanation:

Question:

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
খ. [math]2 \pi[/math]
গ. [math]4 \pi[/math]
ঘ. [math]8 \pi[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]8 \pi[/math]

Solution:
[math]secx[/math]
 এর মৌলিক পর্যায় [math]2 \pi, \sec \frac{x}{4}[/math]
 এর মৌলিক পর্যায় হবে [math]\frac{2 \pi}{\frac{1}{4}}=8 \pi[/math]


Explanation:

Question #393 (ID: 398285)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: BAF Shaheen college, Jessore
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]5 \tan \theta[/math] [math]=4[/math] হলে [math]\frac{5 \sin \theta-3 \cos \theta}{\sin \theta+2 \cos \theta}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{5}{14}[/math]
B. [math]\pm \frac{5}{12}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{5}{13}[/math]
D. [math]\pm \frac{5}{13}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\frac{5}{14}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{4}{5}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta=\frac{4}{\sqrt{41}}[/math]
 এরং [math]\cos \theta=\frac{5}{\sqrt{41}}[/math]
এখন, [math]\frac{5 \sin \theta-3 \cos \theta}{\sin \theta+2 \cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{5 \frac{4}{\sqrt{41}}-3 \frac{5}{\sqrt{41}}}{\frac{4}{\sqrt{41}}+2 \cdot \frac{5}{\sqrt{41}}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{5}{\sqrt{41}}}{\frac{14}{\sqrt{41}}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{5}{14}[/math]

[Image]


Explanation:

Question #395 (ID: 398287)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Ghatail Cantonment Public School & College
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \alpha+\sec \alpha=\frac{5}{2}[/math] হলে [math]\cos \alpha=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]2[/math]
B. [math]1[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
D. [math]0[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\cos \alpha+\sec \alpha=\frac{5}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \alpha+\frac{1}{\cos \alpha}=\frac{5}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow2 \cos ^{2} \alpha+2=5 \cos \alpha[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{2} \alpha-5 \cos \alpha+2=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{2} \alpha-4[/math]
 [math]\cos \alpha-\cos[/math]
 [math]\alpha+2=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \alpha[/math]
 [math](\cos \alpha-2)[/math]
 [math]-(\cos \alpha-2)=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(\cos \alpha-2)[/math]
 [math](2 \cos \alpha-1)=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \alpha=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math][|\cos \alpha| \leq 1][/math]


Explanation:

Question #409 (ID: 398278)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Dhaka City College
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও:

একটি বৃত্তকলার কেন্দ্রে উৎপন্ন কোণ [math]45^{\circ}[/math] এবং বৃত্তটির ব্যাস [math]12[/math] সে.মি.

Question #419 (ID: 398272)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: CITY COLLEGE
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


উদ্দীপকের বৃত্তের চিহ্নিত অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল কত একক?

Options:
A. [math]25 \pi+75[/math]
B. [math]25+25 \pi[/math]
C. [math]75 \pi+25[/math]
D. [math]75 \pi-25[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]75 \pi+25[/math]

Solution:
চিহ্নিত অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল,[math]=[/math]
 বৃত্তের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]– 2 × OAB[/math]
 বৃত্তকলার ক্ষেত্রফল [math]+\triangle \mathrm{OBP}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \pi \times(10)^{2}-2[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{\pi \times(10)^{2} \times 45^{\circ}}{360^{\circ}}+\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\times 10 \cos \left(45^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\times 10 \sin[/math]
 [math]\left(45^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 100 \pi-25[/math]
 [math]\pi+25[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 75 \pi+25[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
সকাল [math]7[/math]টা [math]15[/math] মিনিটের সময় ঘড়ির ঘণ্টা ও মিনিটের কাঁটার মধ্যবর্তী কোণ কত?

ক. [math]120^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]150^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]127.5^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]115.5^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]127.5^{\circ}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\theta=\left|\frac{11 \times \mathrm{M}-60 \times \mathrm{H}}{2}\right|^{\circ}[/math]
 [ [math]M =[/math]
 মিনিট; [math]H =[/math]
 ঘণ্টা [math]][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\left|\frac{11 \times 15-60 \times 7}{2}\right|^{\circ} \\=\left|\frac{165-420}{2}\right|^{\circ} \\=\left|\frac{-255}{2}\right|^{\circ}=127.5^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]

Question #428 (ID: 398264)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও:


[Image]


চিত্রে [math]O[/math] কেন্দ্রবিশিষ্ট বৃত্তে [math]C D=10 \mathrm{~cm}[/math]

ছায়াঘেরা অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল কত?

Options:
ক. [math]7.13 \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]
খ. [math]12.5 \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]
গ. [math]19.63 \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]28.54 \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]7.13 \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]

Solution:
[math]OAB[/math]
 বৃত্তকলার ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{\pi \times 5^{2}}{4}=\frac{25 \pi}{4} \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]
 [math]\triangle O A B[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} \times 5 \times 5=12.5 \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ছায়াঘেরা অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\left(\frac{25 \pi}{4}-12.5\right)=7.13 \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Correct Answer: D.<br/><img src="https://app.nexes.ai/storage/question-bank-images/2025/08/images2fhsc20math201st2020paper20panjeeri20guide20part220chapter206100_1755581958_ahqhHSSD.png" alt="undefined"><br/>

[math]\sin ^{2} x[/math] এর লেখ মূলবিন্দুগামী হবে এবং x অক্ষের উপরে অবস্থান করবে ।

Question #431 (ID: 398259)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
একটি ত্রিভুজের তিনটি কোণের অনুপাত [math]6:8:10[/math] হলে—

i. ক্ষুদ্রতম কোণটি [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]

ii. বৃহত্তম কোণটি [math]\frac{5 \pi}{12}[/math]

iii. ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী

উপরের বাক্যগুলির মধ্যে কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. ii ও iii
গ. i ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
ধরি, ত্রিভুজের তিনটি কোণ, [math]6x, 8x[/math]
 ও [math]10x[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]6 x+8 x+10 x=\pi \quad \therefore x=\frac{\pi}{24}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ক্ষুদ্রতম কোণ [math]=6 \times \frac{\pi}{24}=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 ও বৃহত্তম কোণ [math]=10 \times \frac{\pi}{24}=\frac{5 \pi}{12}[/math]
অপর কোণ [math]=8 \times \frac{\pi}{24}=\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #435 (ID: 398255)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Nexes Solutions
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]8[/math] টা [math]15[/math] মিনিটের সময় ঘণ্টার কাটা ও মিনিটের কাটার মধ্যবর্তী কোণ কত?

Options:
ক. [math]127.5^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]142.5^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]150^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]157.5^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]157.5^{\circ}[/math]

Solution:
ঘন্টার কাঁটা এবং মিনিটের কাঁটার মধ্যে কোণ নির্ণয়ের সূত্র[math]= (30[/math]
 ঘন্টা [math]11[/math]
 মিনিট [math]/2)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=30 \times 8-15 \times 11 / 2 \\=240-165 / 2 \\=240-82.5 \\=157.5^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
সুতরাং, সঠিক উত্তরটি [math]157.5^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii

ক. [math]1[/math]

গ. [math]1+\sqrt{2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]1+\sqrt{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]1+\sqrt{2}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sin ^{2} x[/math]
 এর সর্বোচ্চ মান [math]= 1[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{f}(\mathrm{x})[/math]
 এর সর্বোচ্চ মান [math]=1+\sqrt{2}[/math]

Question #455 (ID: 398232)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin \theta+\cos \theta=\sqrt{2}[/math] হলে, [math]0 \leq \theta \leq \frac{\pi}{2}[/math] ব্যবধিতে [math]\theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
B. $\frac{\pi}{6} $
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sin \theta+\cos \theta=\sqrt{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\frac{\sin \theta}{\sqrt{2}}+\frac{\cos \theta}{\sqrt{2}}=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta \cdot \cos \frac{\pi}{4}+\cos \theta \cdot \sin \frac{\pi}{4}=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \left(\theta+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)=\sin \frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \theta +\frac{\pi}{4}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \theta=\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\pi}{4} \\\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{4} \end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #457 (ID: 398234)

Question:

[Image]


[math]\mathrm{AB}=6 \mathrm{~cm},[/math] চাপ [math]\mathrm{BE}=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{2} \mathrm{~cm}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{3 \pi}{2} \mathrm{~cm}[/math]
C. [math]\pi \mathrm{cm}[/math]
D. [math]2 \pi \mathrm{cm}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\frac{\pi}{2} \mathrm{~cm}[/math]

Solution:

 [math]\therefore B E=S=\pi \theta=3 \times 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=3 \times\left(30 \times \frac{\pi}{180}\right)^{c}[/math]
 [math]\left[1^{\circ}=\frac{\pi}{180^{\circ}}\right][/math]
 [math]=\frac{\pi}{2} \mathrm{~cm}[/math]

Question #459 (ID: 398230)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A[/math] ও [math]B[/math] সূক্ষ্মকোণ, [math]\sin A=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math] এবং [math]\sin B=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math] হলে এর মান কত হবে ?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2 \sqrt {2}}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]\sqrt{3}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sin A=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}},[/math]
 [math]\quad \tan A=1[/math]
 [math]\sin B=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2},[/math]
 [math]\quad \tan B=\sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan A \tan B=\sqrt{3}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #460 (ID: 398227)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\theta<90^{\circ}[/math] এবং [math]3 \tan \theta=4[/math] হলে, [math]\frac{3 \sin \theta+5 \cos \theta}{\sin \theta+\cos \theta}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{27}{7}[/math]
B. $\frac{7}{27} $
C. [math]\frac{29}{7}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{7}{29}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\frac{27}{7}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}3 \tan \theta=4 \\\tan \theta=\frac{4}{3}\end{array}[/math]

[Image]
[math]\sin \theta=\frac{4}{5},[/math]
 [math]\cos \theta=\frac{3}{5}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{3 \sin \theta+5 \cos \theta}{\sin \theta+\cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{3 \cdot \frac{4}{5}+5 \cdot \frac{3}{5}}{\frac{4}{5}+\frac{3}{5}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{12+15}{5}}{\frac{7}{5}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{27}{7}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. [math]2 \sqrt{3}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{2+\sqrt{6}}{\sqrt{6}}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{3}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{\sqrt{2}}{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{3}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}},[/math]
 [math]\cot \theta=\sqrt{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \theta+\cot \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}+\sqrt{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1+2}{\sqrt{2}}=\frac{3}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]

Question #466 (ID: 398217)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\left(\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta \tan \theta+\sec ^{2} \theta \cot \theta\right)[/math] এর সমান –

Options:
A. [math]2 \sin \theta \cos \theta[/math]
B. [math]\sin \theta \cos \theta[/math]
C. [math]2 \sec \theta \operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]
D. [math]\sec \theta \operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]2 \sec \theta \operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]

Solution:
[math]\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta \cdot \tan \theta+\sec ^{2} \theta \cot \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sin ^{2} \theta}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}+\frac{1}{\cos ^{2} \theta}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sin \theta \cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]+\frac{1}{\sin \theta \cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2}{\sin \theta \cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sec \theta \operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]


Explanation:

Question #467 (ID: 398218)

Question:
[math]\theta[/math] সূক্ষ্মকোণ এবং [math]\tan \theta=\frac{3}{4}[/math] হলে, [math]\frac{\sin \theta-\cos \theta}{\sin \theta+\cos \theta}[/math] এর মান—

Options:
A. [math]7[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{7}[/math]
C. [math]-\frac{1}{7}[/math]
D. [math]-7[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]-\frac{1}{7}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\tan \theta=\frac{3}{4}\Rightarrow \frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}=\frac{3}{4} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin \theta-\cos \theta}{\sin \theta+\cos \theta}=\frac{3-4}{3+4}=\frac{-1}{7}=-\frac{1}{7}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{11 \pi}{12}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{11 \pi}{900}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{11 \pi}{4320}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{11 \pi}{2160}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{11 \pi}{4320}[/math]

Solution:

 [math]\left(27+\frac{30}{60}\right)^{\prime}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{55}{2}\right)^{\prime}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{55}{2} \times \frac{1}{60}\right)^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{11}{24}\right)^{0}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{17}{24} \times \frac{\pi}{180}\right)^{c}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{11 \pi}{4320}\right)^{c}[/math]

Question #473 (ID: 398213)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
পাশের সমকোণী ত্রিভুজ থেকে [math](\sin \theta+\cos \theta)[/math] এবং [math](\tan \theta+\cot \theta)[/math] এর অনুপাত হবে—


[Image]


Options:
ক. [math]3: 7[/math]
খ. [math]25: 12[/math]
গ. [math]84: 125[/math]
ঘ. [math]7: 25[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]84: 125[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sin \theta=\frac{3}{5}[/math]
 [math]\tan \theta=\frac{3}{4}[/math]
 [math]\cos \theta=\frac{4}{5} \quad \cot \theta=\frac{4}{3}[/math]
 [math]\frac{\sin \theta+\cos \theta}{\tan \theta+\cot \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{3}{5}+\frac{4}{5}}{\frac{3}{4}+\frac{4}{3}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{7}{5}}{\frac{9+16}{12}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{7}{5}}{\frac{25}{12}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{7}{5} \times \frac{12}{25}=84: 125[/math]


Explanation:

Question #477 (ID: 398209)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


ছায়াঘেরা অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল কত একক ?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{4 \pi}{3}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{4 \pi}{3}-4[/math]
গ. [math]4-\frac{4 \pi}{3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{4 \pi}{3}+4[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\frac{4 \pi}{3}-4[/math]

Solution:
এখানে, [math]\theta=30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(30 \times \frac{\pi}{180}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 রেডিয়ানবৃত্তকলা [math]\text { OPQ }[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} r^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \times 4^{2} \times \frac{\pi}{6}=\frac{4 \pi}{3}[/math]
 বর্গ এককআবার, [math]\triangle O P Q[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রফল[math]=\frac{1}{2} r^{2} \sin \theta=\frac{1}{2} \times 4^{2} \times \sin 30^{\circ}=4[/math]
 বর্গ একক[math]\therefore[/math]
 ছায়াঘেরা অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল=(বৃত্তকলা [math]OPQ[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রফল) [math]-(\triangle \mathrm{OPQ}[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রফল)[math]=\left(\frac{4 \pi}{3}-4\right)[/math]
 বর্গ একক

Explanation:

Question #481 (ID: 398203)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin B=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\cos C=\frac{1}{2}[/math] হলে—

[math]\text { i. } \cos B=\frac{1}{2}[/math] [math]\text { ii. } \sin \mathrm{C}=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math] [math]\text { iii. } \tan B \cdot \sqrt{\sec ^{2} C-1}=3[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক ?

Options:
A. i ও ii
B. i ও iii
C. ii ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:

[Image]
[math]\sin B=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 চিত্র-১ হতে পাই, [math]\cos B=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 এবং [math]\tan B=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{1}=\sqrt{3}[/math]
আবার, [math]\cos C=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
চিত্র-২ হতে পাই, [math]\sin C=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 এবং [math]\sec C=\frac{2}{1}=2[/math]
(iii) [math]\tan \mathrm{B} \sqrt{\sec ^{2} \mathrm{C}-1}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3} \sqrt{2^{2}-1}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3} \sqrt{4-1}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3} \cdot \sqrt{3}=3[/math]


Explanation:

Question #482 (ID: 398204)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও:

একটি চাকা [math]114m[/math] পথ যেতে [math]5[/math] বার ঘুরে ।

চাকার ব্যাসার্ধ কত মিটার?

Options:
ক. [math]2.63[/math]
খ. [math]3.63[/math]
গ. [math]3.78[/math]
ঘ. [math]2.97[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]3.63[/math]

Solution:
চাকা [math]1[/math]
 বার ঘুরলে [math]=2 \pi r[/math]
 দূরত্ব অতিক্রম করেচাকা [math]5[/math]
 বার ঘুরলে [math]=(5 \times 2 \pi)[/math]
 দূরত্ব অতিক্রম করেপ্রশ্নমতে, [math]5 \times 2 \pi r=114\Rightarrow r=\frac{114}{5 \times 2 \pi} \therefore r=3.63[/math]
 মি.

Explanation:

Question #485 (ID: 398196)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


চিত্রে [math]1+\sin 2 \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{4}{5}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{8}{5}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{49}{25}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{25}{41}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{49}{25}[/math]

Solution:
চিত্র-১ হতে পাই, [math]\sin \theta=\frac{3}{5}[/math]
 এবং [math]\cos \theta=\frac{4}{5}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 1 +\sin 2 \theta=\sin ^{2} \theta+\cos ^{2}[/math]
 [math]\theta+2 \sin \theta \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (\sin \theta+\cos \theta)^{2}=\left(\frac{3}{5}+\frac{4}{5}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \left(\frac{3+4}{5}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{7}{5}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{49}{25}[/math]

[Image]


Explanation:

Question #487 (ID: 398198)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sqrt{\frac{\sec \theta-1}{\sec \theta+1}}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\sec \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]
B. [math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta[/math]
C. [math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta+\cot \theta[/math]
D. [math]\cot \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sqrt{\frac{\sec \theta-1}{\sec \theta+1}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{(\sec \theta-1)(\sec \theta-1)}{(\sec \theta+1)(\sec \theta-1)}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sqrt{\frac{(\sec \theta-1)^{2}}{\sec ^{2} \theta-1}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sec \theta-1}{\tan \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sec \theta}{\tan \theta}-\frac{1}{\tan \theta}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\left(\frac{1}{\cos \theta}\right)}{\left(\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}\right)}-\cot \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sin \theta}[/math]
 [math]-\cot \theta[/math]
 [math]=\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\sin \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta=2[/math] হলে [math]\sin ^{n} \theta+\operatorname{cosec}^{n} \theta=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]1[/math]
B. [math]2[/math]
C. [math]n[/math]
D. [math]2n[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]2[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sin\theta+\operatorname{cosec}\theta=2[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta+\frac{1}{\sin \theta}=2 \\\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \theta+1=2 \sin \theta \\\Rightarrow \sin \theta-2 \sin \theta+1=0 \\\Rightarrow(\sin \theta-1)^{2}=0\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #495 (ID: 398192)

Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important

Question:
[math]\sec \theta=2[/math] হলে [math]\frac{1-\tan ^{2} \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{3}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{-1}{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]-\frac{1}{2}[/math]

Solution:
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\sec \theta=2[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{1-\tan ^{2} \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\sec ^{2} \theta+1}{\sec ^{2} \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2-2^{2}}{2^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #496 (ID: 398193)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{f}(\mathbf{x})=2+\sqrt{\sin ^{2}(x)+1}[/math] এর সর্বনিম্ন মান কত হবে?

Options:
A. [math]2[/math]
B. [math]3[/math]
C. [math]4[/math]
D. [math]5[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]3[/math]

Solution:
দেওয়া আছে, [math]f(x)=2+\sqrt{\sin ^{2}(x)+1}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{f}(0)[/math]
 [math]=2+\sqrt{\sin ^{2}(0)+1}[/math]
 [math]=2+\sqrt{0+1}[/math]
 [math]=2+1[/math]
 [math]=3[/math]
যা, [math]f(x)[/math]
এর সর্বনিম্ন মান ।

Explanation:

Question:
একটি বৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ [math]3[/math] সে.মি.। কেন্দ্রে [math]270^{\circ}[/math] কোণ উৎপন্নকারী চাপের দৈর্ঘ্য কত সে.মি.?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{9 \pi}{2}[/math]
খ. [math]9 \pi[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\frac{9 \pi}{2}[/math]

Solution:
[math]r = 3[/math]
 সে.মি. এবং [math]\theta=270^{\circ}=\frac{270 \pi}{180}=\frac{3 \pi}{2}[/math]
চাপ [math]S=r \theta=3 \times \frac{3 \pi}{2}=\frac{9 \pi}{2}[/math]
 সে.মি.

Question #498 (ID: 398185)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sec A=\frac{5}{3}[/math] হলে [math]\sin ^{2} A-\cos ^{2} A=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{25}{7}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{7}{25}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{14}{25}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{25}{14}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\frac{7}{25}[/math]

Solution:
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\sec \mathrm{A}=\frac{5}{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin A=\frac{4}{5}[/math]
 এবং [math]\cos A=\frac{3}{5}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \sin ^{2} A-\cos ^{2} A=\left(\frac{4}{5}\right)^{2}-\left(\frac{3}{5}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{16}{25}-\frac{9}{25}=\frac{16-9}{25}=\frac{7}{25}[/math]

[Image]


Explanation:

Question #499 (ID: 398186)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
এক ব্যক্তি [math]26[/math] মি. ব্যাস বিশিষ্ট বৃত্তাকার মাঠের পরিধির উপর দিয়ে [math]\frac{13 \pi}{6}[/math] মি. দূরত্ব অতিক্রম করলে অতিক্রান্ত অংশটি কেন্দ্রে কত রেডিয়ান কোণ উৎপন্ন করে?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{\pi}{3}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{\pi}{8} .[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]

Solution:
ব্যাস = 26 মি.[math]\therefore[/math]
 ব্যাসার্ধ, [math]r=\frac{26}{2}=13[/math]
 মি. [math]\therefore[/math]
 চাপের দৈর্ঘ্য, [math]S=\frac{13 \pi}{6}[/math]
 মি.আমরা জানি, [math]S=r \theta\Rightarrow \frac{13 \pi}{6}=13 \theta \therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]

Question #500 (ID: 398184)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos ^{2} \theta=\frac{(a-b)^{2}}{4 a b}[/math] সমীকরণে [math]a-b=\sqrt{a b}[/math] এবং 0 <6 < হলে [math]0<\theta<\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
B. [math]90^{\circ}[/math]
C. [math]45^{\circ}[/math]
D. [math]0^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]60^{\circ}[/math]

Solution:
দেওয়া আছে, [math]a-b=\sqrt{a b} \quad[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos ^{2} \theta=\frac{(a-b)^{2}}{4 a b}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \theta=\frac{(\sqrt{a b})^{2}}{4 a b}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \theta=\frac{a b}{4 a b}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \theta=\left(\frac{1}{2}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\cos 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=60^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #502 (ID: 398170)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]x=\frac{1+\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}[/math] হয় তবে [math]\frac{1}{x}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1-\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\cos \theta}{1-\sin \theta}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1+\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\sin \theta}{1+\cos \theta}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\frac{1-\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\frac{1}{x}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos \theta}{1+\sin \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos \theta(1-\sin \theta)}{(1+\sin \theta)(1-\sin \theta)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos \theta(1-\sin \theta)}{1-\sin ^{2} \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]10[/math] ফুট উঁচু একটি খুঁটি কত মাইল দূরে [math]15^{\prime \prime}[/math] কোণ উৎপন্ন করে?

Options:
ক. [math]0.0072[/math]
খ. [math]0.4339[/math]
গ. [math]26.04[/math]
ঘ. [math]1561.08[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]26.04[/math]

Solution:
[math]10=r \times 15^{\prime \prime}=r \times \frac{15^{\circ}}{60 \times 60}=r \times \frac{15 \times \pi}{60 \times 60 \times 180}[/math]
 [math]\therefore r=\frac{10 \times 60 \times 60 \times 180}{15 \times 3 \times 1760 \times \pi}=26.04[/math]
 মেইলNote: [math]1[/math]
 মাইল [math]=3 \times 1760[/math]
 ফুট ।

Question #508 (ID: 398178)

Question:
কোনো ত্রিভুজের কোণগুলো যথাক্রমে [math]x^{\circ}, 100^{\circ}[/math] ও [math]\frac{11 \pi}{36}[/math] হলে x এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]25^{\circ}[/math]
খ. [math]45^{\circ}[/math]
গ. [math]55^{\circ}[/math]
ঘ. [math]60^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]25^{\circ}[/math]

Solution:
ত্রিভুজের কোণগুলো যথাক্রমে [math]x^{\circ}, 100^{\circ}[/math]
 এবং [math]\frac{11 \pi}{36}=[/math]
 [math]\left(\frac{11 \pi}{36} \times \frac{180}{\pi}\right)[/math]
 [math]=55^{\circ}[/math]
আমরা জানি, ত্রিভুজের ত্রিকোণের সমষ্টি [math]=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x^{\circ}+100^{\circ}+55^{\circ}=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=180^{\circ}-155^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore x^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=25^{\circ}[/math]

ঘ. [math]7.5^{\circ}[/math]

Solution:

 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \left|\left(\frac{11}{2} \times 15-30 \times 3\right)^{\circ}\right| \\\Rightarrow \left|\left(82.5-90^{\circ}\right)\right|=\left|-7.5^{\circ}\right|=7.5^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ঘণ্টা ও মিনিটের কাঁটার মধ্যবর্তী কোণ [math]7.5^{\circ}[/math]

Question:
একটি সুপারী গাছ ঝড়ে [math]8[/math] ফুট উচ্চতায় ভেঙে গোড়া থেকে [math]6[/math] ফুট দূরত্বে মাটি স্পর্শ করলে গাছটির উচ্চতা কত ফুট?

Options:
ক. [math]12[/math]
খ. [math]14[/math]
গ. [math]18[/math]
ঘ. [math]35[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]18[/math]

Solution:
মনে করি, গাছটির উচ্চতা = x ফুট।[math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এ পীথাগোরাসের উপপাদ্যপ্রয়োগ করে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}(\mathrm{BC})^{2}=(\mathrm{BA})^{2}+(\mathrm{AC})^{2} \\\Rightarrow (x-8)^{2}=6^{2}+8^{2} \\\Rightarrow x^{2}-16 x-36=0 \\\Rightarrow x^{2}-18 x+2 x-36=0 \\\Rightarrow x(x-18)+2(x-18)=0 \\\Rightarrow (x-18)(x+2)=0 \text {, } \\\therefore x=18 \quad[x+2 
eq 0] \\\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 গাছটির উচ্চতা [math]18[/math]
 ফুট।
[Image]

Question:
[math]\sec \alpha-\tan \alpha=\frac{5}{2}[/math] হলে [math]\sec \alpha+\tan \alpha=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{5}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{2}{5}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{3}{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{5}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\frac{2}{5}[/math]

Solution:
আমরা জানি, [math]\sec ^{2} \alpha-[/math]
 [math]\tan ^{2} \alpha=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (\sec \alpha+\tan \alpha)[/math]
 [math](\sec \alpha-\tan \alpha)=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow (\sec \alpha+\tan \alpha)[/math]
 [math]\cdot \frac{5}{2}=1 \quad[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sec \alpha+\tan \alpha[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2}{5}[/math]

[math]f(x)=\tan ^{201}\left(3 x+\frac{2 \pi}{3}\right)[/math] এবং [math]g(x)=10 \sec ^{69}\left(9 x+\frac{\pi}{3}\right)[/math] [math]g(x)[/math] এর মৌলিক পর্যায় কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{2 \pi}{9}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{\pi}{9}[/math]

Solution:
[math]g(x)[/math]
-এর ঘাত বিজোড়মৌলিক পর্যায় [math]=\frac{2 \pi}{xr}[/math]
এর সহগ[math]=\frac{2 \pi}{9}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]2 P Q=\sqrt{3} R Q[/math] হলে, [math]\cos \theta=[/math] কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \cos \alpha[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}} \sin \theta[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \tan \alpha[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \sin \alpha[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \cos \alpha[/math]

Solution:
[math]\cos \theta=\frac{P Q}{P R}=\frac{P Q}{R Q} \times \frac{R Q}{P R}=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \cos \alpha[/math]

Question #518 (ID: 398162)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও:


[Image]


[math]ABC[/math] বৃত্তের [math]AC[/math] ব্যাস এর দৈর্ঘ্য [math]10[/math] সে.মি ।

ছায়াকৃত অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল কত বর্গ সে.মি.?

Options:
ক. [math]50 \pi-\frac{25 \sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{25 \pi}{2}-\frac{25 \sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
গ. [math]50 \pi-\frac{25 \sqrt{3}}{8}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{25 \pi}{2}-\frac{25 \sqrt{3}}{8}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\frac{25 \pi}{2}-\frac{25 \sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} \times A B \times A C[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \times 10 \sin 30^{\circ} \times 10 \cos 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{25 \sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 বর্গ সে.মি.অর্ধবৃত্ত ABC এর ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{25 \times \pi}{2}[/math]
 বর্গ সে.মি.[math]\therefore[/math]
 ছায়াকৃত অংশের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{25 \pi}{2}-\frac{25 \sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 বর্গ সে.মি.

Question:

[Image]


চিত্রে [math]OCD[/math] বৃত্তকলার ক্ষেত্রফল [math]12[/math] বর্গ সে.মি. এবং চাপ [math]AB = 6[/math] সে.মি.

[math]\theta[/math] = কত রেডিয়ান?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{3}{2}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{2}{3}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]2[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\frac{2}{3}[/math]

Solution:

 [math]\therefore 12=\frac{1}{2} \cdot 6^{2} \cdot \theta\Rightarrow \theta=\frac{24}{36}=\frac{2}{3}[/math]

Question:

[Image]


চিত্রে [math]OCD[/math] বৃত্তকলার ক্ষেত্রফল [math]12[/math] বর্গ সে.মি. এবং চাপ [math]AB = 6[/math] সে.মি.

[math]OAB[/math] বৃত্তকলার ক্ষেত্রফল কত বর্গ সে.মি.?

Options:
ক. [math]15[/math]
খ. [math]21[/math]
গ. [math]27[/math]
ঘ. [math]54[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]27[/math]

Solution:
চাপ [math]s=r \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 6=\text { r. } \frac{2}{3} \quad \therefore r=9[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{OAB}[/math]
 বৃত্তকলার ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} \cdot 9^{2} \cdot \frac{2}{3}=27[/math]
 বর্গ সে.মি.

Question #521 (ID: 398155)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


চিত্র থেকে-

i. [math]\cot \theta[/math] এর মান [math]2+\sqrt{3}[/math]

ii. [math]OA[/math] এর মান [math]-5(\sqrt{6}+\sqrt{2})[/math]

iii. [math]\operatorname{cosec} 2 \theta[/math] এর মান [math]2[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i ও ii
B. ii ও iii
C. i ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\sin \theta=\frac{A B}{O A}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow O A=\frac{A B}{\sin \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{A B}{-\sin \left(270^{\circ}-195^{\circ}\right)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{-5}{-\sin 75^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{5}{\sin \left(45^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{5}{\sin 45^{\circ} \cos 30^{\circ}+\cos 45^{\circ} \sin 30^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{5}{\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}+\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \times \frac{1}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{5}{\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}}}=\frac{10 \sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{3}+1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{10 \sqrt{2}(\sqrt{3}-1)}{3-1}[/math]
 [math]=5(\sqrt{6}-\sqrt{2})[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 (ii) নং' সঠিক নয়

Explanation:

Question #525 (ID: 398159)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :

একটি [math]12[/math] ইঞ্চি ব্যাসবিশিষ্ট পিৎজার [math]8[/math]টি সমান স্লাইস আছে এবং পিৎজার প্রতি বর্গইঞ্চির ভর [math]3[/math] গ্রাম ।

পিৎজার প্রতি স্লাইসের ভর কত গ্রাম?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{27 \pi}{2}[/math]
খ. [math]27 \pi[/math]
গ. [math]810[/math]
ঘ. [math]3240[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\frac{27 \pi}{2}[/math]

Solution:
প্রতি স্লাইসের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} \times r^{2} \times \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \times 6^{2} \times \frac{2 \pi}{8}=\frac{9 \pi}{2}[/math]
 বর্গ ইঞ্চি[math]\therefore[/math]
 প্রতি স্লাইসের ভর [math]=\frac{9 \pi}{2} \times 3[/math]
 গ্রাম [math]=\frac{27 \pi}{2}[/math]
 গ্রাম

Explanation:

Question #526 (ID: 398151)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \frac{\theta}{2}=1[/math] এবং [math]\cos A=\frac{3}{5}[/math] হলে-

[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{i. } \sin (\theta+A)=\frac{4}{5}\\\text{ii. } \tan (2 A+\theta)=-\frac{7}{24}\\\text{iii. } \sec \left(A+\frac{\theta}{2}\right)=-5 \sqrt{2}\end{array}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i ও ii
B. ii ও iii
C. i ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos A=\frac{3}{5} \\\sin A=\frac{4}{5} \\\tan A=\frac{4}{3}\end{array}[/math]

[Image]
[math]\tan \left(\frac{\theta}{2}\right)=1=\tan \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\theta}{2}=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 [math]\text { (i) } \sin (\theta+A)[/math]
 [math]=\sin \theta \cdot \cos A+\cos \theta \cdot \sin A[/math]
 [math]=1 \cdot \frac{3}{5}+0 \cdot \frac{4}{3}=\frac{3}{5}[/math]


Explanation:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
একটি সাইকেলের চাকার ব্যাস [math]1m[/math]। চাকাটি প্রতি মিনিটে [math]20[/math] বার আবর্তিত হলে—

(i). চাকাটির পরিধি [math]100 \pi[/math] সে.মি.

(ii) প্রতি মিনিটে অতিক্রান্ত দূরত্ব [math]= 20m[/math]

(ii) গতিবেগ [math]=\frac{\pi}{3} \mathrm{~m} / \mathrm{s}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
চাকাটির পরিধি [math]=\pi \mathrm{d}=\pi .1 \mathrm{~m}=100 \pi[/math]
 সে.মি.প্রতি মিনিটে অতিক্রান্ত দূরত্ব [math]=20 \times \pi \times 1[/math]
 [math]=20 \pi[/math]
 মি.[math]\therefore[/math]
 গতিবেগ [math]=\frac{20 \pi}{60} \frac{\mathrm{m}}{\mathrm{s}}=\frac{\pi}{3} \mathrm{~m} / \mathrm{s}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #536 (ID: 398129)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]5 \tan \theta=4[/math] হলে [math]\frac{5 \sin \theta-3 \cos \theta}{\sin \theta+2 \cos \theta}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{5}{14}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{14}{5}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{14}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{3}{14}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\frac{5}{14}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{4}{5}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta=\frac{4}{\sqrt{41}}[/math]
 এবং [math]\cos \theta=\frac{5}{\sqrt{41}}[/math]
এখন, [math]\frac{5 \sin \theta-3 \cos \theta}{\sin \theta+2 \cos \theta}=\frac{5 \cdot \frac{4}{\sqrt{41}}-3 \cdot \frac{5}{\sqrt{41}}}{\frac{4}{\sqrt{41}}+2 \cdot \frac{5}{\sqrt{41}}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\frac{5}{\sqrt{41}}}{\frac{14}{\sqrt{41}}}=\frac{5}{14}[/math]

[Image]


Explanation:

Question #537 (ID: 398130)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos x-\sin x=-\sqrt{2}[/math] সমীকরণটির [math]\left(\frac{\pi}{2}, \pi\right)[/math] ব্যবধিতে সমাধান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]0[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{3 \pi}{4}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{3 \pi}{4}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\cos x-\sin x=-\sqrt{2}[/math]
 [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cos x-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \sin x=-1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow, \cos \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\cos x-\sin[/math]
 [math]\frac{\pi}{4} \sin x=-1[/math]
 [math]\cos \left(x+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)=-1[/math]
 [math]\therefore x+\frac{\pi}{4}=(2 n+1) \pi[/math]
 [math]x=0[/math]
 হলে [math]x+\frac{\pi}{4}=\pi[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow, x=\pi-\frac{\pi}{4} .[/math]
 [math]=3 \pi / 4[/math]


Explanation:

Question #538 (ID: 398131)

Question:
[math]f(\theta)=\cos 2 \theta-\sin 2 \theta[/math] হলে [math]\theta[/math] এর কোন মানের জন্যে [math]f(\theta)=0[/math] হবে?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{\pi}{8}[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]\frac{\pi}{8}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos 2 \theta-\sin 2 \theta=0 \\\Rightarrow \sin 2 \theta=\cos 2 \theta \\\Rightarrow \tan 2 \theta=1=\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{8}\end{array}[/math]

Question:
[math]\sec \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta=0[/math] হলে [math]\cos \theta[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{1}{\cos \theta}-\frac{1}{\sin \theta}=0 \Rightarrow \sin \theta-\cos \theta=0 \\\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{4} \therefore \cos \frac{\pi}{4}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\end{array}[/math]

Question #544 (ID: 398137)

Question:
[math]y=\sec (489 x)[/math] এর ডোমেন কত ?

Options:
ক. [math]\mathbb{R}-\left\{\frac{2 \pi}{978}, n \in \mathbb{Z}\right\}[/math]
খ. [math]\mathbb{R}-\left\{\frac{(2 n+1) \pi}{978} ; n \in \mathbb{Z}\right\}[/math]
গ. [math]\mathbb{R}-\left\{\frac{n \pi}{489} ; n \in \mathbb{Z}\right\}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\mathbb{R}-\left\{\frac{2 n \pi}{489} ; n \in \mathbb{Z}\right\}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\mathbb{R}-\left\{\frac{(2 n+1) \pi}{978} ; n \in \mathbb{Z}\right\}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sec (489 x)=\frac{1}{\cos (489 x)} \\\cos (489 x) 
eq 0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\cos (489 x) 
eq \cos (2 n+1) \frac{\pi}{2} \text {; }[/math]
 যেখানে [math]\mathrm{n} \in \mathbb{Z}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 489 x 
eq \frac{(2 n+1) \pi}{2} \\\therefore x 
eq \frac{(2 n+1) \pi}{978}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ডোমেন [math]=\mathbb{R}-\left\{\frac{(2 n+1) \pi}{978} ; n \in \mathbb{Z}\right\}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\cot \theta=-\frac{4}{3}[/math] এবং [math]0 \leq \theta \leq \pi[/math] হলে [math]\frac{\sec (-\theta)+\cos \theta}{\sin \theta-\tan \theta}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{20}{27}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{27}{20}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{-41}{27}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{-27}{41}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{-41}{27}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\cot \theta=\frac{-4}{3}[/math]
 এবং [math]0 \leq \theta \leq \pi[/math]
 হলে[math]\begin{array}{l}\sec (-\theta)=\sec \theta=\frac{5}{-4} \\\cos \theta=\frac{-4}{5} \\\sin \theta=\frac{3}{5} \\\tan \theta=\frac{-3}{4} \\\therefore \frac{\sec (-\theta)+\cos \theta}{\sin \theta-\tan \theta}=\frac{-\frac{5}{4}-\frac{4}{5}}{\frac{3}{5}+\frac{3}{4}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\frac{-25-16}{20}}{\frac{27}{20}}=\frac{-41}{27} \\\end{array}[/math]

[Image]

Question #552 (ID: 398117)

[Image]


[math]A B=6 \mathrm{~cm}[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{BC}=\frac{\pi}{2} \mathrm{~cm}[/math] হলে [math]BOC[/math] বৃত্তকলার ক্ষেত্রফল নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4} \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{\pi}{2} \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{3 \pi}{4} \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{4 \pi}{3} \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{3 \pi}{4} \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]

Solution:
[math]s=r \theta\Rightarrow \theta=\frac{s}{r}=\frac{\frac{\pi}{2}}{\frac{6}{2}}=\frac{\pi}{6}=30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore B O C[/math]
 বৃত্তকলার ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{\pi r^{2} \theta}{360^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\pi \cdot 3^{2} \cdot 30}{360}=\frac{3 \pi}{4} \mathrm{~cm}^{2}[/math]

Question:
একটি চাকার ব্যাস [math]100[/math] সে.মি. হলে [math]10[/math] সে.মি. যেতে চাকাটি কত ডিগ্রি ঘুরবে?

Options:
ক. [math]5^{\circ} 13^{\prime}[/math]
খ. [math]11^{\circ} 27^{\prime}[/math]
গ. [math]11^{\circ} 46^{\prime}[/math]
ঘ. [math]12^{\circ} 50^{\prime}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]11^{\circ} 27^{\prime}[/math]

Solution:
চাকার পরিধি [math]100[/math]
 সে.মি.[math]\therefore[/math]
 চাকাটি [math]10[/math]
 সে.মি. যেতে ঘুরবে [math]=\frac{360^{\circ} \times 10}{100 \pi}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 11^{\circ} 27^{\prime}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\cot \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta=\frac{1}{x}[/math] হলে [math]\cot \theta+\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{1}{x}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{x^{2}}[/math]
C. [math]x[/math]
D. [math]-x[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]-x[/math]

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\operatorname{cosec}^{2} \theta-\cot ^{2} \theta=1 \\\Rightarrow (\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta)(\operatorname{cosec} \theta+\cot \theta)=1 \\\Rightarrow \operatorname{cosec} \theta+\cot \theta=-x\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #558 (ID: 398123)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \theta+\sec \theta=2[/math] হলে [math]\cos ^{n} \theta-\sec ^{n} \theta=?[/math]

Options:
A. [math]-1[/math]
B. [math]0[/math]
C. [math]1[/math]
D. [math]2[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]0[/math]

Solution:
[math]\cos \theta+\frac{1}{\cos \theta}=2 \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos ^{2} \theta+1}{\cos \theta}=2 \\\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \theta-2 \cos \theta+1=0 \\\Rightarrow(\cos \theta-1)^{2}=0 \\\Rightarrow \cos \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos ^{n} \theta-\sec ^{n} \theta[/math]
 [math]=(1)^{n}-\frac{1}{1^{n}}=1-1=0[/math]


Explanation:

Question #559 (ID: 398124)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \theta[/math] কে [math]\tan \theta[/math] এর মাধ্যমে প্রকাশ করলে নিচের কোনটি হবে?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{ \pm 1}{\sqrt{2+\tan ^{2} \theta}}[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{ \pm 1}{\sqrt{1-\tan ^{2} \theta}}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{ \pm 1}{\sqrt{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\frac{ \pm 1}{\sqrt{\tan ^{2} \theta-1}}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{ \pm 1}{\sqrt{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sec ^{2} \theta-\tan ^{2} \theta=1 \\\Rightarrow \sec ^{2} \theta=1+\tan ^{2} \theta \\\Rightarrow \sec \theta= \pm \sqrt{1+\tan ^{2} \theta} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos \theta}= \pm \sqrt{1+\tan ^{2} \theta} \\\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\frac{ \pm 1}{\sqrt{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #560 (ID: 398125)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sqrt{\frac{1-\cos \theta}{1+\cos \theta}}[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\cot \theta-\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]
B. [math]\sin \theta-\tan \theta[/math]
C. [math]\tan \theta-\sin \theta[/math]
D. [math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta[/math]

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sqrt{\frac{1-\cos \theta}{1+\cos \theta}}=\sqrt{\frac{(1-\cos \theta)^{2}}{1-\cos ^{2} \theta}} \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{\frac{(1-\cos \theta)^{2}}{\sin ^{2} \theta}}=\frac{1-\cos \theta}{\sin \theta} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sin \theta}-\frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}=\operatorname{cosec} \theta-\cot \theta\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #561 (ID: 398126)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \theta+\cot \theta=[/math] কত ?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{2}{\sin 2 \theta}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{2}{\cos 2 \theta}[/math]
C. [math]\sin 2 \theta[/math]
D. [math]\cos 2 \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\frac{2}{\sin 2 \theta}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}+\frac{\cos \theta}{\sin \theta}=\frac{\sin ^{2} \theta+\cos ^{2} \theta}{\sin \theta \cos \theta} . \\\Rightarrow \frac{2}{2 \sin \theta \cos \theta}=\frac{2}{\sin 2 \theta}\end{array}[/math]

Explanation:
